Tonk is the game for you.\r\n\r\nIt can also be known as Tunk.\r\n\r\nObjective of Tonk is to eliminate your cards by forming them into ‘spreads’, meaning either 3 or 4 identical cards, or 3 or more sequentially in the same suit.
